msg:Very new, very close to the scenic spot.

Transportation-
Nishan is in Nishan Town, on the outskirts of Qufu City. Take a taxi on the main road, about 35 minutes, 60 yuan, 22 kilometers.
The hotel has a free shuttle bus to Nishan Holy Land, which is very convenient to return to the hotel after watching the night show.

Dining-
The Chinese restaurant stops accepting orders for dinner at 9 o'clock, so you can come back to eat at your leisure after watching the night show.
The breakfast is rich and will be added until the guests leave.

Facilities-
The garden view room is also very large, in the new Chinese style.
The toiletries are complete, the facilities are very new, and the water supply and drainage are very strong.

Service-
Basically in line with expectations, the scenic spot program list will be sent to guests every day.
Remind guests to book a return taxi in advance, and the hotel will also help if they cannot call a taxi temporarily.

After checking in, the hotel butler will actively add WeChat and send the scenic spot performance and experience activity schedule and bus pick-up schedule every day...
The hotel has a bus to take tourists to the scenic spot at a fixed point. It takes 5 minutes to drive to the entrance of the scenic spot. After the tour, the bus will pick you up at a fixed point...
Guests staying in the hotel can enter the scenic spot twice. We checked in on the afternoon of the 4th and went to the scenic spot to play. After watching the fireworks show, light show and drone show, we took the bus back to the hotel at 8:40 pm. After dinner the next morning, we went to the scenic spot again...
The buffet is also very rich and tastes good...
The overall stay is very comfortable, worry-free, and the environment is beautiful. The staff is warm and hospitable. It is recommended to stay at Binshe Hotel when visiting Nishan Holy Land...
